function getParameterByName(a) {
    a = a.replace(/[\[]/, "\\[").replace(/[\]]/, "\\]");
    var c = new RegExp("[\\?&]" + a + "=([^&#]*)"),
        b = c.exec(location.search);
    return b == null ? "" : decodeURIComponent(b[1].replace(/\+/g, " "));
}
